COVID-19

On New Year's Eve 2019

The World Health Organization receives a warning from China. Several unusual cases of pneumonia have been diagnosed in Wuhan City.

Unaware of what is about to begin

The world celebrates the new year 2020 as usual. At this point it's impossible to imagine that an unknown virus is about to revolutionize our lives.

In the beginning of January

Researchers find a new coronavirus. Later, the virus gets the name Sars-Cov-2.

January 11th

China reports the first death and shortly thereafter the virus spreads to other countries in Asia.

Shortly after

WHO announces that the new virus is a threat only in China. The world stays calm.

January 27th

The virus has already spread outside of Asia to the United States, France and Canada.

Januray 30th

WHO declares coronavirus to be a Public Health Emergency of Global Concern.

The beginning of February

Looks hopeful, but after the holidays the situation quickly escalates. Holidaymakers spread the virus from the middle Europe to many other countries.

By the end of February

The virus has spread to over 60 countries. Countries in Europe start to act. Normal air traffic begins to stall.

In mid-March

Europe becomes the epicentre of the pandemic. The United States closes its doors to Europeans. Many states declare a state of emergency. Health care systems start to overload.

By the end of March

The virus is all over the world.
